Garuda-Purana
Part 1

Based on the edition Bombay : Venkatesvara Steam Press (or a reprint thereof)


Input by members of the SANSKNET-project
(www.sansknet.org)



This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding.
Consequently, many word boundaries are not marked by spaces.
The Nagari e-text follows the layout and graphic appearance of the printed 
edition very closely. It even adds blanks when a line break cuts through 
a word or compound.
These and other irregularities cannot be standardized at present.

After many corrections, the text is in need of further proof reading!

÷rãgaruóamahàpuràõam- 3
såta uvàca  /
iti rudràbjajo viùõoş ÷u÷ràva brahmaõo muniş  /
vyàso vyàsàdahaü vakùyehaü te ÷aunaka naimiùe  // GarP_1,3.1 //
munãnàü ÷çõvatàü madhye sargàdyaü devapåjanam  /
tãrthaü bhuvanako÷aü ca manvantaramihocyate  // GarP_1,3.2 //
varõà÷ramàdidharmà÷ca dànaràjàdidharmakàş  /
vyavahàro vrataü vaü÷à vaidyakaü sanidànakam  // GarP_1,3.3 //
aïgàni pralayo dharmakàmàrthaj¤ànamuttamam  /
saprapa¤caü niùprapa¤caü kçtaü viùõornigadyate  // GarP_1,3.4 //

vàsudevaprasàdena sàmarthyàti÷ayairyutaş  // GarP_1,3.5 //
bhutvà harervàhanaü ca sargàdãnàü ca kàraõam  /
devànvijitya garuóo hyamçtàharaõaü tathà  // GarP_1,3.6 //
cakre kùudhà hçtaü yasya brahmàõóamudare hareş  /
yaü dçùñvà smçtamàtreõa nàgàndãnàü ca saükùayaş  // GarP_1,3.7 //

garuóaş sa haristena proktaü ÷rãka÷yapàya ca  // GarP_1,3.8 //

bhairava uvàca  /
nityaklinnàmatho vakùye tripuràü bhuktimuktidàm  /
oü hrãü àgaccha devi aiü hrãü hrãü rekhàkàraõam  /
oü hrãü kledinã bhaü namaş madanakùobhiõà tathà  /
ai yaü yaü krãü và guõarekhayà hrãü madanàntare ca  /
